The central paper proposes travel time prediction using probe-car data with AR/state space models, while neighboring papers focus on outlier detection (ABOD, eigenspace methods, hybrid frameworks), anomaly detection in networks/web systems, distributed data mining, and dynamic syslog analysis, collectively highlighting diverse approaches to time-series analysis and anomaly detection in complex datasets.
The paper demonstrates efficient SQL implementation of K-means clustering, while related works explore OLAP in DBMS using SQL/UDFs and compare SQL/MapReduce for large-scale data mining.
The paper justifies heuristic document preprocessing (IDF, normalization, log transformations) to enhance naive Bayes and multinomial mixture clustering for text tasks, while neighboring works focus on efficient algorithms (topic modeling, relational learning, graph-based prediction, association rule mining, clustering like BIRCH, behavioral targeting, multi-query optimization, recommendation systems, wavelet histograms, collective inference, query optimization, power network prediction, and sampling-based summaries) across data mining, ML, and optimization domains.
The paper explores machine learning for disease classification using metabolomic data, while related works focus on privacy-preserving methods for clustering, association rule mining, and regression analysis on vertically partitioned data.
